# Prometheus Metrics Exposition Pattern Across Kubernetes and Grafana

## Your Task

Find the Go source files in both kubernetes/kubernetes and grafana/grafana that implement the Prometheus metrics exposition pattern: where metrics are registered using the Prometheus client_golang library, how metric collectors are organized, and where the `/metrics` HTTP endpoint is configured to expose them. Compare how both projects structure their metrics infrastructure.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain. Both Kubernetes and Grafana use the Prometheus client_golang library to expose internal metrics, but they organize their metrics registration and exposition differently. Your goal is to map these patterns across both codebases.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/grafana--v11.4.0.

```json

```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Symbol identification**: Correct symbol names and locations?
- **Keyword presence**: Did you mention key concepts (metrics registry, collectors, exposition)?

         // For reference: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/blob/v0.9.2/prometheus/gauge.go#L190-L208\n    79          //\n    80          // In contrast, the Vec behavior in this package \"symbol\": \"NewMetricsOptions\"}\n  ],\n  \"chain\": [],\n  \"text\": \"Both kubernetes/kubernetes (v1.32.0) and grafana/grafana (v11.4.0) use the Prometheus client_golang library to expose internal metrics via a /metrics HTTP endpoint, but they organize their metrics registration and exposition infrastructure quite differently.\\n\\n## Kubernetes: Layered KubeRegistry Abstraction\\n\\nKubernetes builds a custom metrics stability framework on top of the raw Prometheus client. The core is in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/`.\\n\\n### Registry Infrastructure\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go`** defines the central `KubeRegistry` interface and its implementation `kubeRegistry`. `KubeRegistry` wraps a `prometheus.Registry` (via the `PromRegistry` embedded field) and adds Kubernetes-specific lifecycle management: metrics can be marked as ALPHA, BETA, or STABLE (`StabilityLevel`), deprecated at a specific version, or hidden. The `NewKubeRegistry()` function creates a new registry, and `newKubeRegistry()` is the internal constructor. Key methods include `MustRegister()`, `CustomMustRegister()` (for `StableCollector` types), and `RawMustRegister()` (deprecated bypass for raw prometheus collectors). The registry also tracks hidden collectors and resettable metrics.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/legacyregistry/registry.go`** provides the global singleton registry (`defaultRegistry`) used by most Kubernetes components. It exposes package-level functions `MustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`, `Register`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, and `DefaultGatherer`. The `Handler()` function returns an `http.Handler` backed by `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)` instrumented with `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler`. The `HandlerWithReset()` variant also supports DELETE to reset metrics. In its `init()`, it registers `collectors.NewProcessCollector` and `collectors.NewGoCollector` (with all runtime metrics) and calls `RegisterMetaMetrics()`.\\n\\n### Metric Types\\n\\nKubernetes wraps all standard Prometheus metric types (`Counter`, `Gauge`, `Histogram`, `Summary`, `GaugeVec`, `CounterVec`, etc.) in its own structs defined in `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/counter.go`, `gauge.go`, `histogram.go`, `summary.go`. These implement the `Registerable` interface (which extends `prometheus.Collector` with `Create(*semver.Version) bool`, `ClearState()`, and `FQName() string`) and use a `lazyMetric` pattern: metric objects are created eagerly but their underlying Prometheus metric is only instantiated when `Create()` is called at registration time. This allows version-based hiding/deprecation.\\n\\nFor custom collectors, `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/collector.go` defines `StableCollector` (extending `prometheus.Collector` with `DescribeWithStability`, `CollectWithStability`, `Create`, `ClearState`, `HiddenMetrics`) and `BaseStableCollector` as a convenient base struct.\\n\\n### HTTP Exposition\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/http.go`** provides `HandlerFor(reg Gatherer, opts HandlerOpts)` and `HandlerWithReset(reg KubeRegistry, opts HandlerOpts)` which wrap `promhttp.HandlerFor`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`** defines `DefaultMetrics` and `MetricsWithReset` structs, each with an `Install(c *mux.PathRecorderMux)` method that registers the `/metrics` endpoint using `legacyregistry.Handler()` or `legacyregistry.HandlerWithReset()`. The `register()` helper calls `Register()` on several subsystem metric packages (apiserver endpoints, etcd3, cacher, flowcontrol, peerproxy, handlers).\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/config.go`** wires this up: when `EnableMetrics` is true, it calls `routes.MetricsWithReset{}.Install(...)` and `slis.SLIMetricsWithReset{}.Install(...)` (if profiling is enabled) or `routes.DefaultMetrics{}.Install(...)` and `slis.SLIMetrics{}.Install(...)`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/app/serve.go`** (`NewBaseHandler`) directly calls `mux.Handle(\\\"/metrics\\\", legacyregistry.Handler())` for controller manager components.\\n\\n**`pkg/kubelet/server/server.go`** registers multiple metric endpoints: `/metrics` via `legacyregistry.Handler()`, `/metrics/cadvisor` via a separate `compbasemetrics.NewKubeRegistry()` with cAdvisor collectors registered via `RawMustRegister`, `/metrics/resource` via another `NewKubeRegistry()` with `collectors.NewResourceMetricsCollector` registered via `CustomMustRegister`, and `/metrics/probes` via yet another registry with prober metrics.\\n\\n### SLI Registry\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/registry.go`** creates a separate `Registry = metrics.NewKubeRegistry()` for SLI (Service Level Indicator) metrics. **`slis/routes.go`** exposes it at `/metrics/slis`. **`slis/metrics.go`** defines `healthcheck` and `healthchecksTotal` metrics and the `Register(registry)` and `ObserveHealthcheck()` functions.\\n\\n### Subsystem Metric Packages\\n\\nKubernetes uses a pattern where each subsystem has its own `metrics.go` file that defines metrics as package-level variables and a `Register()` function (called once via `sync.Once`) that calls `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` on each metric. Examples:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/workqueue/metrics.go`: registers workqueue metrics and sets `workqueue.SetProvider(prometheusMetricsProvider{})`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/controllers/metrics.go`: `ControllerManagerMetrics` with `Register()` calling `legacyregistry.MustRegister(controllerInstanceCount)`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/restclient/metrics.go`: registers REST client latency, size, result, retry metrics in `init()`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/clientgo/leaderelection/metrics.go`: registers leader election metrics in `init()` and sets `leaderelection.SetProvider(prometheusMetricsProvider{})`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/feature/metrics.go`: registers `kubernetes_feature_enabled` gauge in `init()`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/version/metrics.go`: registers `kubernetes_build_info` gauge in `init()`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/meta/metrics.go`: defines `RegisteredMetrics`, `DisabledMetricsTotal`, `HiddenMetricsTotal` counters\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/clientgo/metrics.go`: blank-imports the above packages to trigger their `init()` functions\\n\\n### Custom Collectors\\n\\n**`pkg/kubelet/metrics/collectors/resource_metrics.go`** implements `ResourceMetricsCollector` (a `StableCollector`) that collects node, pod, and container CPU/memory/swap metrics from the kubelet's resource analyzer. **`pkg/kubelet/metrics/collectors/cri_metrics.go`** implements `criMetricsCollector` (also a `StableCollector`) that dynamically fetches metric descriptors from the CRI runtime and collects pod sandbox metrics. Both implement `DescribeWithStability` and `CollectWithStability`.\\n\\n---\\n\\n## Grafana: Wire-Injected Prometheus Registerer/Gatherer\\n\\nGrafana uses the standard `prometheus.Registerer` and `prometheus.Gatherer` interfaces directly (no custom wrapper), injected via the Wire dependency injection framework.\\n\\n### Registry Infrastructure\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/service.go`** is the central metrics service. `ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (the Kubernetes legacy registry's underlying registerer, since Grafana embeds some k8s components). `ProvideGatherer()` returns a `multiRegistry` that combines a `addPrefixWrapper` around `legacyregistry.DefaultGatherer` (which prefixes non-`grafana_`/`go_` metrics with `grafana_`) and `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`. `ProvideService(cfg, reg)` calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all core Grafana metrics.\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/wireset.go`** defines `WireSet = wire.NewSet(ProvideService, ProvideRegisterer, ProvideGatherer)` and `WireSetForTest` for test injection.\\n\\n### Metric Definitions\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/metrics.go`** defines all core Grafana metrics as package-level variables (e.g., `MInstanceStart`, `MPageStatus`, `MApiStatus`, `MAlertingResultState`, `MStatTotalDashboards`, etc.) using standard `prometheus.NewCounter`, `prometheus.NewGauge`, `prometheus.NewHistogram`, `prometheus.NewSummary`, and their Vec variants. The `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` function calls `reg.MustRegister(...)` with all of them. `SetBuildInformation(reg, version, revision, branch, buildTimestamp)` registers `grafana_build_info` and `grafana_build_timestamp` gauge vecs. `SetEnvironmentInformation(reg, labels)` registers `grafana_environment_info`.\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/frontendmetrics.go`** defines `FrontendMetrics` map and `initFrontendMetrics(r)` which calls `registerFrontendHistogram` for browser performance metrics (boot load time, first paint, etc.).\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/metricutil/utils.go`** provides helpers `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` to pre-initialize counters at zero for all label combinations.\\n\\n**`pkg/infra/metrics/graphitebridge/graphite.go`** implements a Graphite bridge that reads from a `prometheus.Gatherer` and pushes metrics to a Graphite server.\\n\\n### HTTP Exposition\\n\\nGrafana exposes `/metrics` in two ways:\\n\\n1. **`pkg/api/http_server.go`** (`HTTPServer.metricsEndpoint`): The main Grafana HTTP server registers a middleware `metricsEndpoint` that intercepts GET requests to `/metrics`. It uses `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true})` where `promGatherer` is the `multiRegistry` from `ProvideGatherer()`. Basic auth can be required via config. The `promGatherer` and `promRegister` are injected into `HTTPServer` via `ProvideHTTPServer`.\\n\\n2. **`pkg/server/instrumentation_service.go`** (`instrumentationService`): A separate lightweight HTTP server (on a configurable port) that serves `/metrics` using `promhttp.Handler()` (which uses `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`). This is used for internal/instrumentation metrics separate from the main API server.\\n\\n### Request Metrics Middleware\\n\\n**`pkg/middleware/request_metrics.go`** (`RequestMetrics`): A middleware that registers `grafana_http_request_in_flight` (gauge) and `grafana_http_request_duration_seconds` (histogram, with optional native histogram support) via `promRegister.MustRegister(...)` and instruments every HTTP request.\\n\\n### Alerting Metrics (ngalert)\\n\\n**`pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/ngalert.go`** defines `NGAlert` as a top-level metrics container that holds sub-metric structs for each alerting component. `NewNGAlert(r prometheus.Registerer)` constructs all sub-metrics by passing the registerer down. `ProvideService()` uses `prometheus.DefaultRegisterer`. Sub-metric constructors use `promauto.With(r).NewXxx(...)` for automatic registration:\\n- `Scheduler` (`scheduler.go`): alert rule evaluation counters/histograms, scheduler timing\\n- `State` (`state.go`): state update/sync duration histograms; exposes `Registerer()` for the state package to register its own collector\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager` (`multi_org_alertmanager.go`): per-org registries via `OrgRegistries`; `AlertmanagerAggregatedMetrics` is a custom collector registered via `r.MustRegister(moa.aggregatedMetrics)`\\n- `Alertmanager` (`alertmanager.go`): wraps alertmanager API metrics with a prefixed registerer via `prometheus.WrapRegistererWithPrefix`\\n- `API` (`api.go`): request duration histogram\\n- `Historian` (`historian.go`): state history write metrics\\n- `RemoteAlertmanager` (`remote_alertmanager.go`): remote AM sync/latency metrics\\n- `RemoteWriter` (`remote_writer.go`): remote write metrics\\n\\n**`pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/util.go`** defines `OrgRegistries` (per-org `prometheus.Registry` map) and the `Instrument` middleware for alerting API request instrumentation.\\n\\n### Other Subsystem Metrics\\n\\n- **`pkg/apiserver/rest/metrics.go`**: Defines `DualWriterStorageDuration`, `DualWriterLegacyDuration`, `DualWriterOutcome`, etc. as package-level `prometheus.HistogramVec` variables; `dualWriterMetrics.init(reg)` registers them.\\n- **`pkg/registry/apis/query/metrics.go`**: `queryMetrics` struct with `newQueryMetrics(reg)` registering datasource request counters.\\n- **`pkg/expr/metrics.go`**: Similar `metrics` struct for server-side expression metrics.\\n- **`pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go`**: `PrometheusMetrics` struct grouping HTTP client metrics; `NewPrometheusMetricsMiddleware(prefix)` creates them, `Register(registry)` registers them.\\n- **`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/metrics_middleware.go`**: `MetricsMiddleware` with `newMetricsMiddleware(promRegisterer, pluginRegistry)` registering plugin request counters/histograms.\\n- **`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/caching_metrics.go`**: Package-level `QueryCachingRequestHistogram`, `ShouldCacheQueryHistogram`, `ResourceCachingRequestHistogram` registered via `prometheus.Register()` in the caching middleware init.\\n- **`pkg/services/apiserver/standalone/options/metrics.go`**: `MetricsOptions` with `ApplyTo` calling `metrics.ProvideRegisterer()` and `metrics.SetBuildInformation()`.\\n\\n## Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Registry abstraction**: Kubernetes wraps Prometheus in a custom `KubeRegistry`/`kubeRegistry` with stability levels, versioned deprecation, and lazy initialization. Grafana uses `prometheus.Registerer`/`prometheus.Gatherer` interfaces directly.\\n\\n2. **Global registry**: Kubernetes uses a single `legacyregistry.defaultRegistry` (a `KubeRegistry`) as the global sink for most metrics. Grafana uses a `multiRegistry` combining the k8s legacy registry gatherer (with `grafana_` prefix wrapping) and `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`.\\n\\n3. **Collector organization**: Kubernetes uses `StableCollector`/`BaseStableCollector` for custom collectors with stability-aware `DescribeWithStability`/`CollectWithStability`. Grafana uses standard `prometheus.Collector` interface.\\n\\n4. **Registration pattern**: Kubernetes subsystems call `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` in `init()` or explicit `Register()` functions. Grafana subsystems receive a `prometheus.Registerer` via dependency injection and call `reg.MustRegister()` or use `promauto.With(r).NewXxx()`.\\n\\n5. **HTTP exposition**: Kubernetes routes `/metrics` through `routes.DefaultMetrics.Install()` or `routes.MetricsWithReset.Install()` which call `legacyregistry.Handler()`. Grafana uses `promhttp.HandlerFor(gatherer, ...)` in `HTTPServer.metricsEndpoint` middleware and `promhttp.Handler()` in the separate `instrumentationService`.\\n\\n6. **Multiple endpoints**: Kubernetes kubelet exposes `/metrics`, `/metrics/cadvisor`, `/metrics/resource`, `/metrics/probes`, and `/metrics/slis` each backed by separate `KubeRegistry` instances. Grafana exposes a single `/metrics` endpoint.\\n\\n7. **Metric stability**: Kubernetes enforces ALPHA/BETA/STABLE stability levels with automatic hiding of deprecated metrics based on binary version. Grafana has no equivalent stability framework.\"\n}\n",
